!Series_title	"A two miRNA classifier differentiates follicular thyroid carcinomas from follicular thyroid adenomas"
!Series_geo_accession	"GSE62054"
!Series_status	"Public on Oct 07 2014"
!Series_submission_date	"Oct 03 2014"
!Series_last_update_date	"Feb 18 2019"
!Series_summary	"The inherent diagnostic limitations of thyroid fine needle aspiration (FNA), especially in the “indeterminate”  category, can be partially overcome by molecular analyses. We aimed at the identification of  miRNAs that could be used to improve the discrimination of indeterminate FNAs. miRNA expression profiling  was performed for 17 follicular carcinomas (FTCs) and 8 follicular adenomas (FAs). The microarray  results underwent cross-comparison using three additional microarray data sets. Candidate miRNAs were  validated by qPCR in an independent set of 32 FTCs and 46 FAs. Sixty-eight differentially expressed miRNAs  were identified. Thirteen miRNAs could be confirmed by cross comparison. A two-miRNA-classifier was  established improving the diagnostic applicability and resulted in a sensitivity of 82% and a specificity  of 49%. We present a classifier that has the potential to be successfully evaluated in cytology material  for its capability to discriminate (mutation negative) indeterminate cytologies and thereby improving  the pre-surgical diagnostics of thyroid nodules."
!Series_overall_design	"miRNA expression profiling was performed for 17 follicular carcinomas (FTCs) and 8 follicular adenomas (FAs). All samples are independent, coming from different patients."
!Series_type	"Expression profiling by array"

!Sample_data_processing	"All of the data sets were normalized with quantile normalization in R/Bioconductor by preprocessCore library. log2 transformation was applied to diminish the effect of skewed microarray intensity distributions. For our data we additionally applied centering around mean miRNA expression values of FTC samples to diminish technical differences between chips. All miRNAs in all four data sets were annotated with miRBase version 20. 2 versions of normalized file are available: one with miRNA annotation and other with probe sequence annotation."
